A repository of the maps for Cube Trains.
Usage: Each of lines of code is a map. To load, set the level ct-cursor-*'s toLoad variable.
Format: Title of map, then map data. unsolved, solved if available

Mainline Maps:
1. Placement: [tutorial]
	See below.
	
2. The third dimension: [tutorial]
	See blow.

How to Make New Maps:
	Duplicate an existing level. In it's .cfg file (in ~/modules/cube_trains/data/level/), with a text editor, remove the line near the end defining the 'toLoad' variable. If the type of the first object in the file (the playable one) is not ct-cursor-edit, make it so.
	Open up Cube Trains from a console. This is important, because CT will print the map to the console since it has no means of saving to the file.
	You should see a bunch of new objects over to your left, in addition to the objects you normally have access to in Cube Trains. Use these to design your level. When you are done, press f3 to save and serialize the level.
	Copy the serialized level from the console window. Recreate the 'toLoad' variable you deleted, and paste the map data in to define it. Now, there will be a few null()s in the level which will prevent it from loading. Replace these with the appropriate data (have a look at a different level for the format). Replace ct-cursor-edit with ct-cursor-play, and there you go.
